  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_bf354bff-1500-45a5-9d73-2f7256dd9f8d'
      });
    }
    
    var initializeSiwa = function() {
      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"
      loadScript(APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL, initAppleId);
    };
    if (typeof AppleID !== "undefined") {
      initAppleId();
    } else {
      initializeSiwa();

    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/198368999?book_show_action=true">Aug 14, 2011</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Shelly Crane" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Shelly Crane" href="/user/show/5614044-shelly-crane">Shelly Crane</a>

          added it

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer198368999" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8254298463083775869">I am soooo excited about this book! The things I have planned for this series are making me anxious. *insert girly giggle* The first book was all about Caleb and Maggie's relationship and coming into their love and book two will not be lacking in that but, it will also be about Maggie coming into her own as an Ace. She is more important that anyone ever imagined and the people they meet, the situations they get into, the decisions that are forced on them and the people who betray them will, hope</span>
  <span id="freeText8254298463083775869" style="display:none">I am soooo excited about this book! The things I have planned for this series are making me anxious. *insert girly giggle* The first book was all about Caleb and Maggie's relationship and coming into their love and book two will not be lacking in that but, it will also be about Maggie coming into her own as an Ace. She is more important that anyone ever imagined and the people they meet, the situations they get into, the decisions that are forced on them and the people who betray them will, hopefully, blow your mind and make you hopping mad and utterly soaked in sweetness at the same time. <br />I will tell you that if you are anxious to see if the imprints are coming back....definately stay tuned :)<br />Thank you readers for all the comments and reviews and posts for Significance. The response was overwhelming and I sincerely hope you enjoy the next installment of the series.<br /><br />Best Wishes and Happy Endings,<br />Shelly Crane</span>

  <span id="freeText10053416472252825180" style="display:none">This book didn't really advance the story much. Bish continued to be annoying, as did Kyle. The supporting characters in the series seem to be there especially to say inane, spiteful, or ignorant things so that the main characters can stroke each other and whisper sweet nothings. <br /><br />Sometimes the actions were inconsistent, like with the double standard with Jen/Bish and Kyle/Lynne - if Lynne's future could be changed by Maggie's actions, then why couldn't Bish/Jen's? That made no sense, and seems to be there simply to up the drama/tension without actually adding anything to the story over all. <br /><br />All the real action happened at the end, which was great when it happened, but made the first part of the book feel long and dull.<br /><br />I will keep reading the series, because I am invested now, and I want to see it through, but I am going to have to take a break because the grammatical and spelling mistakes from the first book continued in this one, and my brain needs a break!</span>

  <span id="freeText2617486958078191647" style="display:none">This book was okay, but there were things that irked me. I feel like the author was trying absolutely too hard to show how much the main character Maggie and her "Significant" Caleb love each other. I understand that the "imprint" that they have makes them this way but its reiterated too much. I am hoping the next book is better because this one sort of dissapointed me. The first book was good but the second is making me think again.</span>

<div id="review_504732789" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/504732789" />
    <a title="Melissa" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/7448090-melissa"><img alt="Melissa" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1407525447p2/7448090.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/504732789?book_show_action=true">Jan 12, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Melissa" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Melissa" href="/user/show/7448090-melissa">Melissa</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="did not like it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">did not like it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7448090-melissa?shelf=yeah-not-so-much-dnf">yeah-not-so-much-dnf</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer504732789" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer562441835878204958">After the first novel I was into the story, a little more on the YA side for me but still I was intrigued by the world of Aces and was loving Caleb. All that good stuff. But then....I started reading Accordance.<br/><br/>And, contrary to the many 5 star reviews, which btw I'm still trying to figure out, this one was uber slow. Actually, it was uber everything - the pacing was painful with the relationship and on the action front. It was dead in the water or overstuffed with filler scenes that didn't add t</span>
  <span id="freeText562441835878204958" style="display:none">After the first novel I was into the story, a little more on the YA side for me but still I was intrigued by the world of Aces and was loving Caleb. All that good stuff. But then....I started reading Accordance.<br /><br />And, contrary to the many 5 star reviews, which btw I'm still trying to figure out, this one was uber slow. Actually, it was uber everything - the pacing was painful with the relationship and on the action front. It was dead in the water or overstuffed with filler scenes that didn't add to the momentum of the plot. I was skippin pages like my life depended on it. This was almost reminiscent of Charlaine Harris' last Sookie book minus the checking of the emails. <br /><br /><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[In addition to this, the characters, whom I really liked in Significance were annoying the everloving shit outta me!! Gahd sakes. You could've made a drinking game out of how many times Caleb told Maggie he loved her and she said it back, how many times he just wants to see her happy and keep her safe, how many bleedin' times this girl is SORRY for all the trouble she "caused", ugh!!! Like a mouse could fart in the room and she's busting out with the tears. Just get over it already, let's get on with your destiny. I really hate being such a harsh critic, especially on indie authors, because I admire, respect and appreciate the balls they have getting their stuff out there. But I always believed in shooting it straight...so here are my peeves:<br /><br />- What makes for a strong story are strong characters, weak is NEVER sexy. Sure, have some initial/occasional self-doubt but after the learning curve, cut it off. Turning your protagonist into a compulsive apologist makes for bad fiction and contradicts where the protagonist is supposed to end up -ultimately a position of power, no? She's supposed to be maturing not regressing to a 13 year old idiot. The story should not be found in the mountain of self-doubt you wish your protagonist to experience over the length of a bible, it should be found in actual challenges in her way and the meat is in how she deals with them (i.e. Night Huntress series by Jeaniene Frost) <br /><br />- Caleb = emasculation. Having him say "I love you" every 10 seconds and pretty much nothing else makes him come off as....a little whipped and one dimensional. Not to mention, more importantly, when I'm reading the L word every page it really loses impact when they do say it, not as meaningful. <br /><br />- Bish - I wanted to chop his head off and feed slowly to my goldfish. I'm not too sure what the point was in making him as ultra annoying as he was. Even the strictest parents wouldn't be that overreactive to a few kisses. Perhaps find a different way to build his forlorn character portrait. Having him ride the heroine that hard about her destined relationship just turns the reader against the character. Honestly I couldn't care less if he gets his HEA and when he does, he'll just be a big hypocrite. <br /><br />- Same for Kyle, thankfully I skimmed to the part where he imprinted and could stop being just as annoying as Bish. <br /><br />- Story was too much centered around Maggie. Although not always the case in general, in Accordance it made me feel something was missing from the story. Everyone was all about her, dealing with her freakouts, soothing her sadness, dancing around to make her happy. I guess it was the characters weren't really their own person, more of a vehicle to allow Maggie to exist and experience life as an Ace, which she spent wishing for the opposite the majority of the book. It was annoying. If you're stuck being a Supernatural with a really hot guy for eternity f***kin suck it up already and get the step on! <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> </span>
  <a data-text-id="562441835878204958" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3024878-donna-book-passion-for-life?shelf=for-review">for-review</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3024878-donna-book-passion-for-life?shelf=ya-paranormal-romance">ya-paranormal-romance</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer251790251" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4212775124969907286"><i>
  <b>He smiled graciously and pressed his nose and cheek to mine with a hand on my jaw. “I'm so in love with you.”</b>
</i><br/><br/>Shelly Crane has done it again and knocked out ANOTHER fantastic novel. <i>Significance</i> was the first book in the series and it literally blew me away and now <i>Accordance</i>; the second book in the series has left me lost for words because of how awesome it was. <br/><br/><i>Accordance</i> starts where Significance finishes and from the start you’re thrown into Maggie’s and Caleb’s wonderful but dangerous li</span>
  <span id="freeText4212775124969907286" style="display:none"><i>
  <b>He smiled graciously and pressed his nose and cheek to mine with a hand on my jaw. “I'm so in love with you.”</b>
</i><br /><br />Shelly Crane has done it again and knocked out ANOTHER fantastic novel. <i>Significance</i> was the first book in the series and it literally blew me away and now <i>Accordance</i>; the second book in the series has left me lost for words because of how awesome it was. <br /><br /><i>Accordance</i> starts where Significance finishes and from the start you’re thrown into Maggie’s and Caleb’s wonderful but dangerous life. Their still trying to get to know on another and even though their completely in love, they are still trying to take steps that a normal couple would take. Like going to a club, going for dinner and wondering about their relationship going to the next level. They are that much stronger as a couple in this book because they finally come into their abilities and it was truly wonderful to watch them explore and test their new abilities. It’s honestly a joy to read about these two and I feel closer to them more than ever. <br /><br />What I enjoyed more about this book was we had a lot more interaction from the secondary characters like Kyle &amp; Jen. I really enjoyed finding more about them and watching their journeys develop. I was absolutely thrilled for Kyle and Lynne, it wasn’t something I expected so it was a nice surprise but what I loved most was Bish and Jen’s story. How heart-breaking! I’ll be honest I don’t really care for Bish all that much, he annoyed me through out this book, being so over protective of Maggie but boy, do I want a happy ending for him. Shelly please give this boy a happy ending! <br /><br />The story its self is as dangerous as ever and with new threats popping up all over the place Maggie and Caleb sure have their work cut out for them. I can not wait to see what happens next because talk about a cliff-hanger! May 2012 cannot come quick enough. <br /><br /><i>A huge thank you to Shelly Crane for giving me the opportunity to review this book.</i> <br /></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer3971318890053960931">Accordance was perfect sequel to <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/11731861.Significance__Significance___1_' title='Significance (Significance, #1) by Shelly Crane' rel='nofollow noopener'>Significance</a>. There were so many unexpected twists and I found myself speechless and surprised quite often during reading this book. I literally <b>could not stop reading</b>, storyline was maximally exciting and my heart was furiously beating most of the time. It is only 2nd book out of 4 and I already love this series so much!<br/><br/>Development of the characters comparing to the first book was pretty visible. Even though Maggie was overwhelmed and freaked out after she learn</span>
  <span id="freeText3971318890053960931" style="display:none">Accordance was perfect sequel to <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/11731861.Significance__Significance___1_" title="Significance (Significance, #1) by Shelly Crane" rel="nofollow noopener">Significance</a>. There were so many unexpected twists and I found myself speechless and surprised quite often during reading this book. I literally <b>could not stop reading</b>, storyline was maximally exciting and my heart was furiously beating most of the time. It is only 2nd book out of 4 and I already love this series so much!<br /><br />Development of the characters comparing to the first book was pretty visible. Even though Maggie was overwhelmed and freaked out after she learnt all that supernatural stuff about herself, I admired her for eventually accepting all that responsibility. I know I would definitely freaked out myself. And I admired Caleb even more for his ability to be patient and always helping and supporting Maggie no matter what. Moreover, the way Caleb and Maggie are connected and able to communicate with each other is probably one of the most fascinating things I have ever read about. And even though Kyle irritated me even more that in the first book, I fell even more in love with rest of the Jacobson family, they are just amazing. <br /><br />This book shows us that everything happens for a reason. Good things, bad things, everything has a meaning. But Mrs. Crane definitely did not make it easy for main characters and I cannot even imagine what else will happen to them in next books in series. <b>If you are YA paranormal lovers, you have to read this series!!!</b></span>

<div id="review_254460228" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/254460228" />
    <a title="Celeste Dailey" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3159713-celeste-dailey"><img alt="Celeste Dailey" src="https://s.gr-assets.com/assets/nophoto/user/f_50x66-6a03a5c12233c941481992b82eea8d23.png" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/254460228?book_show_action=true">Jan 01, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Celeste Dailey" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Celeste Dailey" href="/user/show/3159713-celeste-dailey">Celeste Dailey</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="did not like it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">did not like it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer254460228" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6153162180529049088">So, since I did enjoy "Signifacance", I was hoping to like "Accordance". I was hoping even more that this book would have better editing than the previous one, but no such luck. I felt the story line dragged a bit and while I do like Caleb and Maggie, I quickly tired of Caleb's, "I would never hurt you" line and Maggie's "This is all my fault" line. Plus, the overall structure is just poor. There are a ton of missing question marks, "their" that should have been "there", and vice versa, and "thr</span>
  <span id="freeText6153162180529049088" style="display:none">So, since I did enjoy "Signifacance", I was hoping to like "Accordance". I was hoping even more that this book would have better editing than the previous one, but no such luck. I felt the story line dragged a bit and while I do like Caleb and Maggie, I quickly tired of Caleb's, "I would never hurt you" line and Maggie's "This is all my fault" line. Plus, the overall structure is just poor. There are a ton of missing question marks, "their" that should have been "there", and vice versa, and "threw" instead of "through". Then there is this scene early on where Maggie and Caleb go surfing. The author writes that they put on wetsuits, but in the next paragraph, Maggie is in her bikini and Caleb is in his shorts. The kicker was that they are in California, and the author describes them surfing in the morning, yet the sun is low over the water turing it orange? I live in California and here out west, the sun SETS over the ocean, so it would only be low over the water in the evening. There are so many errors in this book that there were times I had to put it down because I was getting so irritated with it all. I did make myself finish it, though. I don't think I'll read the third book as I'm not sure I can sit through anymore poor writing even if the story is good. </span>
  <a data-text-id="6153162180529049088" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>


      <div class="reviewFooter uitext buttons">

<div id="review_228449523" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/228449523" />
    <a title="Morgan" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5637577-morgan"><img alt="Morgan" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1373569756p2/5637577.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/228449523?book_show_action=true">Oct 28, 2011</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Morgan" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Morgan" href="/user/show/5637577-morgan">Morgan</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5637577-morgan?shelf=4-stars">4-stars</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer228449523" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1003632736616875429"><a href='http://www.readingeatinganddreaming.blogspot.com' rel='nofollow noopener'>CLICK HERE TO READ MORE REVIEWS AT READING, EATING AND DREAMING I WAS BLAIR WALDORF</a><br/><br/>If you haven’t started reading the Significance series yet then you should fix that immediately. It’s a phenomenal paranormal romance series for young adults. It’s exciting, romantic, suspenseful and dramatic. The first two books, Significance and Accordance, are now available on Amazon.com, and the third book, Defiance, will be released May 2012. I am not sure how many books will make up the complete series, but </span>
  <span id="freeText1003632736616875429" style="display:none"><a href="http://www.readingeatinganddreaming.blogspot.com" rel="nofollow noopener">CLICK HERE TO READ MORE REVIEWS AT READING, EATING AND DREAMING I WAS BLAIR WALDORF</a><br /><br />If you haven’t started reading the Significance series yet then you should fix that immediately. It’s a phenomenal paranormal romance series for young adults. It’s exciting, romantic, suspenseful and dramatic. The first two books, Significance and Accordance, are now available on Amazon.com, and the third book, Defiance, will be released May 2012. I am not sure how many books will make up the complete series, but I know that Defiance will not be the last book in the series.<br /><br />Accordance, the second novel in the Significance series, picks up exactly where Significance left off. Everything that I loved about Significance can be found in this novel: humor, romance, shocking developments, drama, and more paranormal revelations. Accordance was just as good as Significance, if not better.<br /><br />If you want a more in depth review, check out my review for Significance. My feelings haven’t changed. :)<br /><br />There were a few surprises in this novel and some confirmations. The only bad thing about this novel is that it ended and I have to wait a really long time for the next book in the series.<br /><br />So far, the Significance series has been a very clean series. The main characters don’t drink alcohol. The language and hook ups are innocent. Maggie has morals, and she sticks to them. Caleb respects Maggie’s wishes, and he doesn’t push her for more even though his body craves hers. Maggie and Caleb also respect their parent’s wishes. I think it’s nice to find a clean novel every now and then. I also read adult romance novels, so squeaky clean isn’t a requirement of mine. However, I like to find a good, clean young adult story every now and then.<br /><br />I gave Accordance by Shelly Crane 4 STARS. This series kicks butt. I strongly recommend this series to young adults. <br /><br />-XOXO<br /><br /><a href="http://www.readingeatinganddreaming.blogspot.com" rel="nofollow noopener">READING, EATING AND DREAMING</a></span>

          </span>

<div id="review_252610662" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/252610662" />
    <a title="Alyssa" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/806430-alyssa"><img alt="Alyssa" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1393794508p2/806430.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/252610662?book_show_action=true">Dec 29, 2011</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Alyssa" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Alyssa" href="/user/show/806430-alyssa">Alyssa</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/806430-alyssa?shelf=paranormal-romance">paranormal-romance</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer252610662" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17381478470084506687">This seemed like more of a transition book than anything else, and it seemed to be lacking in both focus and plot. Not much really went on, there was not much action or movement along, and it felt like time was just dragging on. There was a section of the middle of the book where I got really frustrated with Maggie. She just seemed so... I don't know. Like too much of a goody two-shoes or something. Too good. Too unreal. Caring too much about other people and not the right people. I didn't like </span>
  <span id="freeText17381478470084506687" style="display:none">This seemed like more of a transition book than anything else, and it seemed to be lacking in both focus and plot. Not much really went on, there was not much action or movement along, and it felt like time was just dragging on. There was a section of the middle of the book where I got really frustrated with Maggie. She just seemed so... I don't know. Like too much of a goody two-shoes or something. Too good. Too unreal. Caring too much about other people and not the right people. I didn't like how they just always had to throw their money around to help all these random people. I didn't like how she was just so loose about telling everyone the Jacobson family's secrets. She was just so careless with her visions and suddenly it seemed like all that talk about secrecy was for nothing. It just didn't even seem in alignment with the story, especially when Maggie was suddenly able to see the visions of others' imprints, when originally those images were supposed to be for those individuals alone. It just seemed so intrusive, like she was invading on something that wasn't even supposed to be her business. And how she always stopped Bish and Jen from happening.<br /><br />I don't know. I just feel like 70% of this book rubbed me the wrong way. I don't like how Maggie dealt with her problems either, why she thought it was okay to do what she did at the concert (don't want to give away spoilers here). It just didn't seem right and this entire novel just seemed so... not right.<br /><br />All in all though I suppose it was still okay. I still like the world, I like Maggie and Caleb together, I like that Kyle finally manned up and became mature, and I'll still read the third book because I want to know what happens, I just wasn't very impressed with this story, as I was with the first one, and it just didn't really seem like much of a story to me. Also, I didn't really work it out in my head but I felt like more time had actually passed in the story since Maggie and Caleb got together than was actually stated at different intervals in the book. I could be wrong though.</span>

          </span>

<div id="review_190178175" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/190178175" />
    <a title="Mandy (I Read Indie) Anderson" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3261049-mandy-i-read-indie-anderson"><img alt="Mandy (I Read Indie) Anderson" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1603247644p2/3261049.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/190178175?book_show_action=true">Jul 26, 2011</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Mandy (I Read Indie) Anderson" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Mandy (I Read Indie) Anderson" href="/user/show/3261049-mandy-i-read-indie-anderson">Mandy (I Read Indie) Anderson</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer190178175" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14016314231286104569">Accordance takes off where Significance left off, with Caleb and Maggie arriving in California for her protection against the Watson's. Just when they thought they have some time to themselves to learn about each other, Kyle and Bish show up to chaperone. Time alone is few are far between now. Bish is there to find out what his sister is hiding, and why everyone is ok with Maggie running off to another state with a guy she just met. And Kyle just won't leave well enough alone.<br/><br/>Maggie is coming to</span>
  <span id="freeText14016314231286104569" style="display:none">Accordance takes off where Significance left off, with Caleb and Maggie arriving in California for her protection against the Watson's. Just when they thought they have some time to themselves to learn about each other, Kyle and Bish show up to chaperone. Time alone is few are far between now. Bish is there to find out what his sister is hiding, and why everyone is ok with Maggie running off to another state with a guy she just met. And Kyle just won't leave well enough alone.<br /><br />Maggie is coming to terms that she is not only an Ace, but that she is also a seer. She can read the minds of those around her, see into their minds, feelings, plans, even see visions. Sure it comes in handy when needing a few seconds to talk to Caleb without Bish learning of what they are, not so handy when all of Kyle's feelings are of his love for her.<br /><br />One day Maggie gets a vision that will affect Aces everywhere. She learns the past mistakes of the clans, the greed and pride they held above all. She also learns the prophecy that she and Caleb are the ones to put an end to it all and bring back what the Virtuoso's once were, caring and giving people. But soon, with everything piling up on her shoulders, all the emotions and responsibilities just becomes to much. Will Maggie be able to live up to what her new family is expecting or will she let them all down?<br /><br />Accordance is so wonderfully written with a story line that is unlike any other. It’s easy to lose yourself in the world that Crane creates. I felt the happiness, the unease and the suspense right along with the characters. And lets not forget the romance, ohhh the romance. Shelly brings back all those memories of first love: the stolen kisses, the dreams you have, the playful touches. My favorite thing about a book is the love story and this author knows how to deliver, in all her works. Accordance is a must read by a brilliant author. You will not be disappointed. <br /><br />﻿<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="14016314231286104569" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer17083090041119160453">If i could , i would have rated it 'Infinity' !!! God this book is sooooooooooo good !! It is the most awesomest book ever .   <span id="freeText17083090041119160453" style="display:none">If i could , i would have rated it 'Infinity' !!! God this book is sooooooooooo good !! It is the most awesomest book ever . I finished it 2 hrs ago and was so speechless that i just didnt know what to say . WOW , AMAZING , FANTASTIC , BREATH-TAKING BEAUTIFUL , i can just go on and on about how good it was . <br />The book starts off exactly where the previous one finished . Our destined love birds Caleb and Maggie , enjoying a quite nice time in California under the scrutiny of their super hot chaperones . But trouble for the couple is not far away and yet again we find ourselves amidst those trouble makers a.k.a 'the bad guys'. <br />This was definitely an emotional rollercoster ride . It was always difficult to chose whether i should happy for someone's gain or sad for something one probably could never have . It literally made me cry at certain points . I dont want to go in revealing a lot here because its definitely an exciting read . And its better to experience all this by reading the book . I totally loved Maggie in this book . She understood what she is and took it really well , instead of constantly whining about it . This book certainly had surprises of their own which , well something that i guessed would not happen but did actually happen !! Again the whole family supporting each other during times of trouble was awesome . I guess thats makes it easier to connect with the characters . They feel so real . Everytime i read a book i treat it as a movie which is playing in my head . Makes reading so much fun . This is one movie i would definitely wanna watch for reel . Hollywood still listening !!!<br />A must read . Cant wait for the third book in this series . Really looking forward to it !!<br />SHELLY CRANE , YOU HAVE OUTDONE YOURSELF . I THOUGHT THE FIRST BOOK WAS BETTER , WELL THIS WAS EVEN BETTER THAN THAT . HATS OFF TO YOU !! YOU ARE ONE OF MY FAVOURITES AUTHOR FROM HERE ON . LOVE YOU LOTS AND THANK YOU FOR SUCH AN AWESOME BOOK :) </span>

<span id="freeTextContainer17832603801913909289">Okay, so if you read my review of book one in the Significance series, you'll understand me when I say that the fifteen-year-old within me won out in even reading the sequel to Significance. <br/><br/>As with the first book, the second one was completely relationship-driven.   <span id="freeText17832603801913909289" style="display:none">Okay, so if you read my review of book one in the Significance series, you'll understand me when I say that the fifteen-year-old within me won out in even reading the sequel to Significance. <br /><br />As with the first book, the second one was completely relationship-driven. With the exception of a brief appearance early on, the bad guys don't even come into the story until it's almost over. <br /><br />Once again, Kyle is the most interesting character (not, mind you, the main character), and the main players seem as obsessed with each other as they were in the first book.<br /><br />Thankfully, the Watsons (plural, not possessive) were mentioned WITHOUT the previously incorrect apostrophe usage this time, though it was slipped in once or twice.<br /><br />Honestly, I am struggling to come up with something new to say that I haven't already mentioned in my review of book 1. I feel even less actually happened in this story than the first one, with the exception of a few supernatural developments.<br /><br />Once again, this story fell short of my expectations. I doubt I'll be reading the third installment in this series... no matter how much my inner teenager begs.</span>

    <div class="section">
      

<div id="review_192760236" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/192760236" />
    <a title="Tee loves Kyle Jacobson" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2566871-tee-loves-kyle-jacobson"><img alt="Tee loves Kyle Jacobson" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1459255542p2/2566871.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/192760236?book_show_action=true">Jul 31, 2011</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Tee loves Kyle Jacobson" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Tee loves Kyle Jacobson" href="/user/show/2566871-tee-loves-kyle-jacobson">Tee loves Kyle Jacobson</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
                  <em>
                    This review has been hidden because it contains spoilers. To view it,
                    <a href="#" onclick="Effect.toggle(&#39;reviewTextContainer192760236&#39;); return false;">click here.</a>
                  </em>
              <span id="reviewTextContainer192760236" class="readable"
                    style="display:none"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16446626314188954309">My Cover Thoughts: I absolutely love this cover. It is of a tree with leaves growing on it. To me the tree signified a new grow and change for the coming season. Change is always good when you’re with the one you love. The saying on the cover is so true. To become what you’re destined to be, you have to first find out who you are.<br/><br/>My Thoughts/Review: In Significance we found out the Maggie and Caleb had imprinted and are soul mates. She is coming to terms with it but is having a hard time because</span>
  <span id="freeText16446626314188954309" style="display:none">My Cover Thoughts: I absolutely love this cover. It is of a tree with leaves growing on it. To me the tree signified a new grow and change for the coming season. Change is always good when you’re with the one you love. The saying on the cover is so true. To become what you’re destined to be, you have to first find out who you are.<br /><br />My Thoughts/Review: In Significance we found out the Maggie and Caleb had imprinted and are soul mates. She is coming to terms with it but is having a hard time because her best friend Kyle wanted to be more than just friends and was upset that Caleb had imprinted with Maggie when he knew how Kyle had felt about her.<br /><br />Then there was Marcus who was upset that The Jacobson clan had imprinted at all and to make matters worse it was with a human girl. That was unheard of and it upset Marcus and his uncle. Marcus and his clan had not imprinted and they longed to find their soul mates to. So Marcus decided he would follow his uncle’s advice and help him hurt Maggie so they could stop her from being with Caleb.<br /><br />In Accordance Maggie is still struggling with her feelings for Caleb and her family. She is still in danger and she just wants to have a normal life with Caleb by having a normal teenage relationship by hanging out, going to the movies and just enjoying Caleb. That is impossible because she and Caleb have gone away for the summer so she does not get hurt again and in leaving they are whisked away to new problems and new advisories. <br /><br />Maggie is starting to understand her abilities and she is also given some new ones. With Caleb by her side she knows she can do anything but what is a girl to do when she has her older protective brother right by her side. Bish does not really know what is going on between Maggie and Caleb and he does not care. All he knows is that his sister was happy one day with no boyfriend and then he comes home to visit and she can’t seem to stay away from this guy. He is upset and wants to know what is going on and he will stop at nothing to find out. While on his quest he finds he is starting to like someone he does not think he can have. So with all this pent up anger what is a big brother to do?<br /><br />You add Kyle to the mix and Bish is totally confused. He knows they have been friends since childhood but he is not so sure why Maggie doesn’t like Kyle in that way when it is clear that Kyle loves Maggie and would do anything to be with her. Kyle makes innuendos and passes at Maggie and Caleb would love nothing more than to kill him but Maggie knows what Kyle is doing and that is to make Caleb mad and jealous so he can feel what Kyle feels. Caleb knew Kyle loved Maggie for all these years and now that they are imprinted Kyle has to sit by and watch Caleb win the girl of his dreams. <br /><br />This story continues on Maggie’s quest to find herself and the truth of what is really going on with the clans. With this quest comes some self searching and her realizing that she is destined to do something great. Can she fulfil the prophecy in time and can she be with Caleb like they were meant to be. Can Maggie help Kyle see what he is doing to her and Caleb is wrong. Can she have her friends and family and still keep this secret she is holding. In the end Maggie must make the ultimate sacrifice. Can she do it??????<br /><br />Memorable Quotes: Kyle and Maggie at the club where Maggie has just had another vision. There were a couple energy ribbons bouncing behind Beck’s head. Oh no, no! What could I do? Everyone was going to see and I couldn’t stop. My body was too worked up. I looked at Kyle helplessly, knowing there was no way to explain or make him understand. And he looked back knowing there was nothing he could do either. I hid my face and took a deep breath. Kyle pulled my face back to look at him with a hand on my cheek and I didn’t think, I just acted, or reacted rather. <br />Then I remembered Caleb and I practiced reigning it in and kissing seemed to have worked, so without any thought to consequences for Kyle or me or Caleb, without any wonder to what Beck would think about seeing me kiss Kyle, without any thought at all really except to keep everyone from seeing what I was… <br />I reached up from my knees on the floor and kissed him. <br />I held his collar for stability and though Kyle’s mind was shocked and unsure, his hands definitely knew what to do. They snaked themselves around my waist and he had an inkling, an after thought really, that there was more to this. That there was a very good reason I was kissing him that had absolutely nothing to do with my wanting him, but he didn’t give a flip at the moment. This was what he had waited for, for two years and he was going to savor it. <br />He kissed nothing like Caleb. His lips felt all wrong and nothing like the love I felt all through me when Caleb took my lips. All I saw and felt was Kyle‟s want and desire for me. With Caleb there was love, protection and adoration mixed in with a need to make me happy and comfortable but with Kyle, he was solely focused on the fact that he‟d wanted me for so long and could never have me. That thing inside me that told me what I was doing was so, so wrong was pulsing and screaming uncomfortably. I pulled back, hoping the short kiss had been enough to stop the uncontrollable Visionary in me. <br />“I’m sorry,” I told him quietly, looking up into his unbridled eyes. <br />I was losing control. I couldn’t think of anything else to do.” <br />“Maggie, what happened?” he asked breathlessly. <br />“I had a…” I looked at Beck sitting there waiting for her own explanation with wide unbelieving eyes and knew I couldn’t give him an answer. Beck’s mind screamed the fact that she was confused at why I was kissing Kyle. “It was nothing.”<br /><br />Advice: This series is a must read! I love Shelly Crane’s writing style and I love how her story draws you in and you can feel each characters emotion and feel their pain.<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="16446626314188954309" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1948201554?book_show_action=true">Mar 24, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Aimee (Getting Your Read On)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Aimee (Getting Your Read On)" href="/user/show/1934633-aimee-getting-your-read-on">Aimee (Getting Your Read On)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1934633-aimee-getting-your-read-on?shelf=ebook-i-own">ebook-i-own</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1934633-aimee-getting-your-read-on?shelf=ya">ya</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1934633-aimee-getting-your-read-on?shelf=paranormal">paranormal</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1948201554" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer18386405369932377580">3.5<br/><br/>The story I love. The characters I love. This book just needs a good editor to take out all the unnecessary stuff. There is too much repetition. Too much of the same thoughts and words coming from the two main characters. Too much space in between, waiting for something else to really happen. This book could be condensed and not loose anything vital. <br/><br/>But, I really am enjoying the story. It's a fun change from the other books I've been reading. I'll be going back for the next book but not quit</span>
  <span id="freeText18386405369932377580" style="display:none">3.5<br /><br />The story I love. The characters I love. This book just needs a good editor to take out all the unnecessary stuff. There is too much repetition. Too much of the same thoughts and words coming from the two main characters. Too much space in between, waiting for something else to really happen. This book could be condensed and not loose anything vital. <br /><br />But, I really am enjoying the story. It's a fun change from the other books I've been reading. I'll be going back for the next book but not quite yet. I need a bit of a breather. :)<br /><br />Content: kissing, innuendo</span>

//<![CDATA[  

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('aXcm9KOCLBkbwVSiVvoynFWbFy5vTkeXCx8m0aC5Bfw1/oANznE9xYBfJAb9i8ZdURUUBZyWOI1whIL84CYT4g==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('TJqkoXhl7Xo+UYujQ4OU1Ou5L3H52d1819cxEor7AwkQEwJYFZb8pqXP+wfo8mAV7zcsWgoBomasTJU/ymQVFw==')})
  }
//]]>
</script>

  <span id="freeText9089293281106113780" style="display:none">Shelly is a NEW YORK TIMES &amp; USA TODAY bestselling author from a small town in Georgia and loves everything about the south. She is wife to a fantastical husband and stay-at-home mom to two boisterous and mischievous boys who keep her on her toes. She hoards paperbacks, devours sweet tea, searches year-round for candy corn, and loves to spend time with her family and friends, go out to eat at new restaurants, site-see in the new areas they travel to, listen to music, and, of course, loves to read, but doesn’t have much time to these days with all the characters filling her head begging to come out.<br /><br />Her own books happen by accident and she revels in the writing and imagination process. She doesn't go anywhere without her notepad for fear of an idea creeping up and not being able to write it down immediately, even in the middle of the night, where her best ideas are born.<br /></span>
